# <a name="release-notes-for-current-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-103">目前通道的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-103">Release notes for Current Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-104">這些版本資訊提供新功能和非安全性更新的相關資訊，這些功能和非安全性更新包含在 Microsoft 365 Apps 企業版、Microsoft 365 Apps 商務版，以及 Project 和 Visio 版的傳統型應用程式訂閱版本的目前通道更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Current Channel updates for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, Microsoft 365 Apps for business, and the subscription versions of the desktop apps for Project and Visio.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-105">我們會變更 Microsoft 365 應用程式的更新通道，包括新增新的更新通道 (每月企業通道)，並變更現有的更新通道名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-105">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-106">如需深入了解，[請閱讀本文](/DeployOffice/update-channels-changes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-106">To learn more, [read this article](/DeployOffice/update-channels-changes).</span></span>

 > [!NOTE]
>
>- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-107">我們通常會在一段時間對「目前」通道推出功能 (有時甚至推出修正程式)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-107">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Current over a period of time.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-108">如果您現在沒有看到如下所述的項目，您可以預期它近期會推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-108">If you don’t see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-109">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-109">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
>- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-110">Microsoft Teams 功能可能會與最新的目前通道中發行的功能不同，因為後者的發行頻率較高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-110">Microsoft Teams features may differ from the latest Current Channel released as they have a more frequent release cadence.</span></span>

## <a name="version-2102-march-18"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-113">版本 2102：3 月 18 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-113">Version 2102: March 18</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-114">*版本 2102 (組建 13801.20360)*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-114">*Version 2102 (Build 13801.20360)*</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT START)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-116">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-116">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-117">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-117">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-118">此變更可修正在某些情況下，執行 SQL Server 傳遞查詢時，可能會導致錯誤訊息指出「無效的 Cursor 狀態」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-118">This change fixes an issue where in some cases running a SQL Server pass through query could result in an error message indicating that there was an "invalid cursor state".</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-119">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-119">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-120">我們已修正會導致雲端設定功能的使用者在新裝置上設定 Outlook 之後，會看到自訂設定遭到預設設定覆寫的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-120">We fixed an issue that caused users of the Cloud Settings feature to see customized settings overridden by default setting after configuring Outlook on a new device.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-121">我們已修正會導致使用者看到較預期更多的簽章的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-121">We fixed an issue that caused users to see more signatures than expected.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-122">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-122">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-123">我們已修正在隱藏段落結尾輸入可能會導致應用程式懸置的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-123">We fixed an issue with typing at the end of a hidden paragraph may result in application hang.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-124">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-124">Office Suite</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-125">已修正使用者在開啟先前開啟的檔案具有未儲存的編輯但現在檔案已遭到刪除時，無法儲存檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-125">Fixed an issue where users are unable to save file when open a previously opened file with edits not saved but now the file has been deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-126">修正之後，使用者將會收到一則友善的訊息，通知他們已刪除該檔案，因此使用者可以選擇捨棄變更，或將檔案另存為新檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-126">After the fix, users will get a friendly message to inform them that the file is deleted, thus user can choose to discard changes, or SaveAs the file.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-127">我們已修正與支援在工作階段 0 中執行的 Office 應用程式相關的可靠性問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-127">We fixed a reliability issue related to support of Office apps running in session 0.</span></span>



[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT END)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-133">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-133">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-135">我們已修正會導致使用者在 Outlook 重新啟動之前，在功能窗格中看不到新增的行事曆顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-135">We fixed an issue that caused users to see newly added calendars fail to appear in the navigation pane until after Outlook had been restarted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-138">我們已修正可能會略過段落的朗讀程式問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-138">We fixed an issue with Narrator which may skips over a paragraph.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-139">我們已修正 RTF 內容控制項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-139">We fixed an issue with Rich text content controls.</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-140">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-140">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-141">已修正在包含數學方程式的文字內使用朗讀程式時可能發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-141">Fixed an issue that could happen when using narrator within text that contains math equations.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-146">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-146">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-147">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-147">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-148">**同時取消隱藏多個工作表：** 不再需要一次取消隱藏一個工作表，可以一次取消隱藏多個隱藏的工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-148">**Unhide many sheets at the same time:** No need to unhide one sheet at a time anymore -- unhide multiple hidden sheets at once.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-149">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-149">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/69f2701a-21f5-4186-87d7-341a8cf53344)

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-150">**改善條件式格式設定對話方塊：**[條件式格式設定] 對話方塊現在可以調整大小，且現在您只要按一下就能複製規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-150">**Improved Conditional Formatting dialogs:** Conditional Formatting dialogs are now resizable, and now you can duplicate the rule with a single click.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-151">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-151">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/fed60dfa-1d3f-4e13-9ecb-f1951ff89d7f)

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-152">**要求使用者套用敏感度標籤：** 當使用者的組織原則要求時，會提示使用者套用敏感度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-152">**Require users to apply sensitivity labels:** Users will be prompted to apply a sensitivity label if their organization's policy requires it.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-153">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-153">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-154">**更新的連絡人清單檢視：** 連絡人清單現在會顯示電子郵件地址，以及更新的相片和文字大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-154">**Updated Contacts list view:** Contacts list now shows email addresses and updated photo and text size.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-155">**使用內建翻譯工具打破語言障礙：** 不再需要翻譯的增益集！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-155">**Break the language barrier with a built-in translator:** Add-ins for translation aren't required anymore!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-156">您現在可以在 Outlook 中使用 Intelligent Translator。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-156">You can now use the Intelligent Translator in Outlook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-157">當您收到另一種語言的郵件時，郵件上會顯示提示，詢問您是否希望 Outlook 將它翻譯為您的預設語言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-157">When you receive a message in another language, a prompt will appear on top of the message asking if you’d like Outlook to translate it to your default language.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-158">您也可以按一下滑鼠右鍵以翻譯特定的文字、片語或整個郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-158">You can also right-click to translate specific words, phrases, or the whole message.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-159">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-159">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/287380e4-a56c-48a1-9977-f2dca89ce93f)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-160">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-160">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-161">**要求使用者套用敏感度標籤：** 當使用者的組織原則要求時，會提示使用者套用敏感度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-161">**Require users to apply sensitivity labels:** Users will be prompted to apply a sensitivity label if their organization's policy requires it.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-162">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-162">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-163">**共用 PowerPoint 檔案時的簡報者檢視畫面**：在會議中共用 PowerPoint 檔案時，簡報者現在會有投影片組中所有投影片的縮圖區域檢視，以便輕鬆進行臨機操作的投影片瀏覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-163">**Presenter View when sharing a PowerPoint file:** When sharing a PowerPoint file in a meeting, the presenter can now a thumbnail strip of all the slides in the deck for easy ad-hoc slide navigation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-164">**佈景主題和圖示更新：** 我們對預設和深色佈景主題色彩和圖示進行了更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-164">**Theming and icon updates:** We have made updates to the default and dark theme colors and to the icon.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-165">**iPad 上的即時活動簡報者支援：** 您可以透過支援的 iPad 裝置在即時活動中進行簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-165">**Live Event Presenter Support on iPad:** You can present in a live event from your supported iPad device.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-166">**使用 Microsoft Forms 讓會議參與者投票：** Teams 會議的投票是可輕鬆探索且順暢的體驗，可協助您進行更吸引人且更具生產力的會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-166">**Poll meeting participants using Microsoft Forms:** Polls for Teams meetings is an easily discoverable and seamless experience that will help you conduct more engaging and productive meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-167">利用由 Microsoft Forms 提供支援的「投票」功能，會議簡報者可以分別在會議之前、期間和之後準備、啟動及評估投票，這一切都可以在 Teams 會議的一個索引標籤下進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-167">With Polls, which is powered by Microsoft Forms, meeting presenters can prepare, launch, and evaluate polls before, during, and after meetings, respectively, all from one place under a tab in the Teams meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-168">身為會議簡報者，您可以將 Forms 應用程式新增為 Teams 會議中的索引標籤，然後從一個位置建立、啟動及評估您的投票。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-168">As a meeting presenter, you can add the Forms app as a tab in the Teams meeting, then create, launch, and evaluate your polls from one place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-169">建立投票以在會議期間啟動，甚至在會議開始之前啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-169">Create polls to be launched during the meeting even before the meeting begins.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-170">然後，在會議之後，您可以選擇在索引標籤中、在匯出的 Excel 活頁簿或在 Forms 應用程式的網頁上評估回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-170">Then, after the meeting, you can choose to evaluate responses in the tab, an exported Excel workbook, or on the web in the Forms app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-171">簡報者有各種不同的控制項，例如啟用匿名回應、關閉投票，以及將結果匯出至 Excel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-171">Presenters have a variety of controls, like enabling anonymous responses, closing polls, and exporting results to Excel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-172">來自任何端點 (行動裝置、網頁、桌面) 的出席者可以在投票出現在會議畫面或會議聊天中時檢視和回答投票，以及即時查看非匿名的投票結果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-172">Attendees from any endpoint (mobile, web, desktop) can view and answer polls as they appear on the meeting screen or in the meeting chat, as well as see non-anonymous poll results in real time.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-173">**會議反應：** 會議反應是在會議中互動的新方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-173">**Meeting reactions:** Meeting reactions are a new way to interact in meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-174">參與者可以傳送反應且反應會以資料流的形式顯示在共用的內容上，以及在傳送該反應的個人上 (如果他們有在會議階段上顯示)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-174">Participants can send reactions and they'll be shown as a stream on content that is shared, and on the individual who sent the reaction if they're displayed on the meeting stage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-175">**桌面用戶端的歷程記錄功能表：** Teams 桌面用戶端中的歷程記錄功能表，可讓您輕鬆回到最近瀏覽過的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-175">**History Menu for desktop client:** The History Menu in Teams desktop client lets you easily get back to recently visited locations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-176">只要將游標停留在桌面用戶端的下一頁或上一頁瀏覽選項上，然後選取位置即可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-176">Simply hover over the forward or backward navigation options in the desktop client and select the location.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-177">也可使用鍵盤快速鍵來開啟功能表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-177">A keyboard shortcut is also available to open the menu.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-178">**適用於美國的 Microsoft Teams 會議室中的 Cortana：** Microsoft Teams 會議室中的 Cortana 語音協助可讓您有不需觸控，即可從會議室撥打號碼、加入或結束會議或新增號碼至會議的體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-178">**Cortana in Microsoft Teams Rooms for US:** Cortana voice assistance in Microsoft Teams Rooms lets you have a touchless experience for calling a number from your conference room, joining or ending a meeting, or adding a number to a meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-179">**遮罩電話號碼：** 我們發佈了新的系統管理員設定，用於在撥入參與者加入會議時遮罩其電話號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-179">**Masking phone numbers:** We released a new admin setting for masking phone numbers for dial-in participants when they join a meeting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-180">系統管理員可以選擇為來自會議中的每個人 (會議召集人除外)、僅來自外部的人員遮罩電話號碼，或是將遮罩功能停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-180">Admins can choose to mask phone numbers from everyone in the meeting (except the organizer), from external people only or have masking disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-181">如果系統管理員選擇停用此設定，將會在會議中完整顯示電話號碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-181">If the admins choose to have this setting disabled, the phone numbers will be displayed fully in the meeting.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-182">(10 月底之前屬於私人發行)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-182">(private release until the end of October)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-183">**行事曆共用：** 我們新增了將頻道新增到行事曆索引標籤的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-183">**Calendar sharing:** We added the ability to add a channel to a calendar tab.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-184">**為在一起模式增加更多場景：** Teams 現已推出可讓會議召集者或簡報者變更在一起模式場景的功能，讓出席者可以一起以不同的體驗顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-184">**Bringing more scenes to Together Mode:** Teams have now introduced the ability for meeting organisers or presenters to change the Together Mode scene allowing attendees to appear in different experiences together.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-186">**單鍵書寫建議：** 只要按一下，就能套用書寫建議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-186">**One-click writing suggestions:** Apply writing suggestions with a single click.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-187">更新的 [編輯器] 窗格讓您輕鬆在建議之間瀏覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-187">The updated Editor pane makes it easy to navigate between suggestions.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-188">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-188">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/1e72a440-89a6-457c-bd76-cd5cea901dc0)<br /><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-189">在[部落格文章](https://insider.office.com/en-us/blog/microsoft-editor-gets-an-upgrade)中查看詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-189">See details in [blog post](https://insider.office.com/en-us/blog/microsoft-editor-gets-an-upgrade)</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-423">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-423">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-424">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-424">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-425">我們已修正在傳送工作的狀態報告時，造成 [收件者] 欄位為空白的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-425">We fixed an issue that caused the To field to be blank when sending a status report on a task.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-426">我們已修正會導致 MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd 事件中斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-426">We fixed an issue that caused the MailItem.BeforeAttachmentAdd event to be broken.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-427">我們新增了一個 RegKey，可讓客戶停用 IDataObject 操作 (例如，拖曳拖放、剪貼簿) 中附件的 FileTime 包含內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-427">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-428">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-428">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-429">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-429">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-430">0 = 不包含 filetimes。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-430">0 = filetimes are excluded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-431">1 = (預設) 包含 filetimes。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-431">1 = (default) filetimes are included.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-432">我們已修正當回覆含有「Azure 資訊保護」保護標籤的郵件時，導致內嵌影像消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-432">We fixed an issue that caused inline images to disappear when replying to a message with a protection label from Azure Information Protection.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-433">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-433">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-434">已修正 Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 會對舊版影片格式 (MPG-1、Mpeg-2) 發生當機的 VBA 問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-434">We have fixed a VBA issue where Slide.Shapes.AddMediaObject2 crashing with legacy video formats (MPG-1,Mpeg-2).</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-435">我們已修正在複製含有新錄製音訊的投影片後，儲存檔案時發生錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-435">We fixed an issue where there is an error when saving the file after duplicating a slide that contains a newly recorded audio.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-436">已修正無法正確開啟部分損壞的 PowerPoint 檔案 (即使在文件修復之後) 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-436">Fixed an issue where some corrupt PowerPoint files were not opening correctly, even after a document repair operation.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-443">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-443">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-444">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-444">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-446">我們新增了一個 RegKey，可讓客戶停用 IDataObject 操作 (例如，拖曳拖放、剪貼簿) 中附件的 FileTime 包含內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-446">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-447">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-447">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-448">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-448">REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-449">0 = 不包含 filetimes。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-449">0 = filetimes are excluded.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-450">1 = (預設) 包含 filetimes。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-450">1 = (default) filetimes are included.</span></span>

### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-472">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-472">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-473">**隨時跟上改變！[日期/時間] 延伸資料類型具有更好的精確度。：** 引進新的和改良的資料類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-473">**Keep up with the times! The Date/Time Extended data type has better precision.:** Introducing a new and improved data type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-474">為加強與 SQL 的語法相容性，並提高包含日期和時間之記錄的詳細資料和層級，我們正在將 DateTime2 資料類型實施到 Access 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-474">To enhance syntax compatibility with SQL, and to increase accuracy and level of detail in records that include dates and times, we’re implementing the DateTime2 data type into Access.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-475">這個額外的日期與時間資料類型，將會包含更大的日期範圍（0001-01-01 到9999-12-31），具有更高的指定時間精準度(以納秒取代秒為單位)，讓您可以提供和執行計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-475">This additional date & time data type will include a larger date range (0001-01-01 through 9999-12-31), with higher-specified time precision (nanoseconds, rather than seconds) that you will be able to provide and perform calculations on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-476">若要啟用，請選取 [新增欄位] > [日期與時間延長]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-476">To enable, select New field > Date & Time Extended.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-477">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-477">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/708c32da-a052-4cc2-9850-9851042e0024)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-522">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-522">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-523">這是此問題的修正：當有增益集在接聽 PresentationBeforeClose 事件並隨著事件處理常式檢查 Presentation.Saved 內容時若關閉文件，儲存提示會以迴圈顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-523">This is a fix for an issue where the save prompt shows in a loop when closing the document when there is an add-in that listens to PresentationBeforeClose event and checks Presentation.Saved property as a part of the event handler.</span></span>


### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-524">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-524">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-525">修正當您將專案從 PWA 儲存到本機 mpp 檔案時，ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent 會對實際上未由使用者變更的資料觸發的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-525">Fixed an issue where when you save a project from PWA to a local mpp file, the ProjectBeforeTaskChangeEvent fires for data that wasn't actually changed by the user.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-526">修正 Project 在開啟以特定方式指定資源分佈的檔案時可能會意外終止的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-526">Fixed an issue where Project may terminate unexpectedly when opening files where resource contours were specified in a certain manner.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-662">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-662">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-663">**合併通話：** 合併通話可讓使用者將使用中的 unheld 1-1 撥入另一個1-1 通話或另一個群組通話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-663">**Call Merge:** Call Merge gives end users the capability to merge their active unheld 1-1 call into another 1-1 call or another group call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-664">這適用於Teams VOIP 通話和 PSTN 通話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-664">This applies to Teams VOIP calls and PSTN calls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-665">**系統管理員可以針對其第一線工作者設定按班表顯示（上班、下班）：** 系統管理員可以設定其第一線工作者使用以班表為基礎的狀態顯示：上班、忙碌中（到班時可以切換）和下班。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-665">**Admins can configure shift-based presence (On shift, Off shift) for their Firstline workers:** Admins can configure their firstline workers to have shift-based presence states: On shift, Busy (can be toggled when on shift), and Off shift.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-666">**在Teams中使用 Cortana 語音技能：** Teams行動裝置的應用程式的Cortana 語音功能, 可協助使用者僅使用口頭自然語言即可執行會議、通訊與共同協作任務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-666">**Cortana voice skills in Teams:** Cortana voice skills in Teams mobile app help users perform meeting, communication and collaboration tasks simply using spoken natural language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-667">使用者可以在Teams應用程式中點擊麥克風按鈕與Cortana交談, 而且當他們困在家務中或遛狗或一般外出需與某人聯繫時, 可以發出諸如“打電話給Megan”或“對我的下一個會議發送訊息”之類的請求.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-667">Users can speak to Cortana by clicking on the microphone button in Teams app and make requests like “Call Megan” or “Send a message to my next meeting” if they need to connect with someone while juggling household chores or walking the dog or generally on the go.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-668">使用者只要說「加入我的下一個會議」即可加入會議，或者詢問「我今天早上有什麼事」來檢查行事曆。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-668">Users can join meetings simply by saying “Join my next meeting” or check their calendar by asking “what do I have this morning”.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-669">在會議或通話中，他們可以從會議主持者的 [溢出] 功能表中調用 Cortana，並執行典型的會議中任務，例如按照姓名或電話號碼（「將 Megan 新增至通話」）、投影片瀏覽（「顯示季度檢閱投影片瀏覽」）或檢視投影片（「移至投影片備忘稿」）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-669">Once in a meeting or a call, they can invoke Cortana from the overflow menu in the meeting stage and perform typical in-meeting tasks like adding people by name or number (“Add Megan to the call”), deck presentation (“present the quarterly review deck”) or navigating slides (“Go to the appendix slide”).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-670">該功能還支持其他功能, 如尋找及共享檔案、搜尋，並通常在Teams應用中導航（與約翰聊天，移至我的未讀取活動，請移至我的表述等等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-670">Other things that the feature supports are finding and sharing files, search, and generally navigating within the Teams app (“Open my chat with John, Go to my unread activity, Go to my mentions etc.).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-671">Teams 的Cortana 對Cortana 企業服務來說說符合對 Cortana 企業服務相同的的企業級隱私、安全性和合規性承諾，並反映在 [線上服務條款（OST）](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products)中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-671">Cortana in Teams meets the same enterprise-level privacy, security, and compliance promises for Cortana enterprise services, as reflected in the [Online Services Terms (OST)](https://www.microsoft.com/licensing/product-licensing/products).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-672">**增加群組交談：** Teams新增了群組聊天中可有250個參與者的功能.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-672">**Group chat increase:** Teams added the ability to now have 250 participants in a group chat.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-673">**按 Shift 加上標籤:** 使用這項功能，系統會自動在小組中的 [Shifts app](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop) 應用程式中, 為人員指派符合其行程和班表的標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-673">**Tagging by Shift:** With this feature, people are automatically assigned tags that match their schedule and shift group name in the [Shifts app](https://support.microsoft.com/office/get-started-in-shifts-5f3e30d8-1821-4904-be26-c3cd25a497d6#bkmk_openshiftsappdesktop) in Teams.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-687">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-687">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-688">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-688">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-689">已解决此問題 - 您現在可以使用 Office 的隨選即用應用程式外的 ODBC 驅動程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-689">This issue has been resolved - you can now use our ODBC driver outside of Office's Click-to-Run applications.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-690">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-690">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-691">修正導致使用者嘗試從次要帳戶建立會議邀請的問題，讓帳戶新增至他們的個人檔案，而不會看到空白的表格: 是欄位而不是其電子郵件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-691">Fixes an issue that caused users who attempted to create a meeting request from a secondary account added to their profile to not see a blank From: field instead of their email address.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-692">已修正新增共用信箱之後，導致使用者無法連線至公用資料夾的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-692">Fixes an issue that caused users to be unable to connect to Public Folders after adding a shared mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-693">解決了當代理人在某些情況下遭到拒絕而導致會議無法從經理的行事曆中移除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-693">Addressed an issue that caused meetings to fail to be removed from a manager's calendar when declined by a delegate in some circumstances.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-749">**建立 PDF 連線：** 連線至、匯入、重新整理 PDF 中的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-749">**Make a PDF connection:** Connect to, import, refresh data from a PDF.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-750">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-750">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/be4330b3-5356-486c-a168-b68e9e616f5a)

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-751">**篩選和排序而不干擾其他人：** 您現在可以排序和篩選您的 Excel 檔案，同時與其他人使用工作表檢視進行共同作業。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-751">**Filter and sort without disrupting others:** You can now sort and filter your Excel file while collaborating with others with Sheet View.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-752">此新功能可防止您在共同撰寫文件時，受到其他使用者的排序和篩選的影響。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-752">This new feature prevents you from being impacted by other user’s sorts and filters while coauthoring the document.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-753">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-753">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/0eea3dc5-d7d1-44c5-a953-25ebfbd6c1a6)

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-755">**在 Excel 中建立來自 Power BI 資料的樞紐分析表：** 您可以在 Excel 中建立樞紐分析表，只要按幾下滑鼠，就能連線到儲存在 Power BI 的樞紐分析表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-755">**Create PivotTables from Datasets in Power BI within Excel:** You can create PivotTables in Excel that are connected to datasets stored in Power BI with a few clicks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-756"> 如此一來，您就能獲得樞紐分析表和 Power BI 的最佳效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-756">Doing this allows you get the best of both PivotTables and Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-757">使用安全 Power BI 資料集的樞紐分析表以計算、摘要及分析資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-757">Calculate, summarize, and analyze your data with PivotTables from your secure Power BI datasets.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-758">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-758">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/31444a04-9c38-4dd7-9a45-22848c666884)<br /><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-759">在[部落格文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)中查看詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-759">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-769">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-769">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-770">**新增簡化的通知設定：** 使用者現在可以使用增強的功能，以更簡單的方式管理其通知設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-770">**New simplified notification settings:** Users can now manage their notifications settings in a more simplified manner with enhanced functionalities.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-771">**Teams 現在支援 Windows 原生通知：** 使用者現在可以選取其偏好的通知傳送方式，即透過 Teams 內建橫幅或 Windows 原生橫幅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-771">**Windows Native Notification are now Supported on Teams:** Users can now select their preferred means of notification delivery, either through teams built in banners or the windows native banners.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-772">**頻道資訊窗格：** 選取頻道標頭中的 [頻道資訊] 圖示時，將開啟一個窗格，其中會顯示頻道資訊的摘要，包括頻道描述、最近的參與者和成員清單，以及系統訊息的新首頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-772">**Channel Info Pane:** When selecting on the "Channel info" icon in the channel header, a pane will open where you will see a summary of channel information including the channel description, a list of recent contributors and members, as well as the new home for system messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-773">**關閉聊天通知的預覽：** 使用者可以變更設定，並管理其聊天通知快顯的預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-773">**Turn off previews for your chat notifications:** Users can change settings and manage previews for their chat notification toasts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-774">**建議的回覆：** 我們新增了讓 Teams 使用者對其交談具備建議的回覆功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-774">**Suggested replies:** We added the ability for Teams users to have a suggested reply to their conversations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-775">這些建議會顯示在聊天訊息的底部 (如果已啟用)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-775">These suggestions will appear at the bottom of a chat message if they are enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-776">它們能讓您快速輕鬆地回覆訊息！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-776">They make replying to messages quick and easy!</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-777">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-777">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-778">**[自動套用] 或 [建議敏感度] 標籤：** Office 可以根據偵測到的敏感性內容來推薦或自動套用靈敏度標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-778">**Auto-apply or recommend sensitivity labels:** Office can recommend or automatically apply a sensitivity label based on the sensitive content detected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-779">**以向量保留文字：** 現在當您在 Excel、Word 和 PowerPoint 中轉換地圖、圖表和其他 SVG 向量等物件時，您可以保留物件中的文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-779">**Retain text in vectors:** Now you can retain the text in maps, charts, and other SVG vectors when converting these objects in Excel, Word, and PowerPoint.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-837">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-837">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-838">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-838">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-839">**較長的檔案名稱：** Windows 桌面版專用 Excel 現在支援使用最多 400 個字元名稱和路徑的 OneDrive/SharePoint 檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-839">**Longer file names:** Excel for Windows desktop now supports OneDrive/SharePoint files with names and paths of up to 400 characters.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-840">**RealTimeData (RTD) 的改進：** 在 Office 365 版本 2002 的每月通道或更新版本中，Excel RealTimeData (RTD) 函數速度比在 Excel 2010 試算表中計算資料還快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-840">**Realtimedata (RTD) improvements:** In Office 365 version 2002 monthly channel and later, Excel's RealTimeData (RTD) function is much faster than Excel 2010 calculating data in the spreadsheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-841">我們在其基礎記憶體和資料結構中移除了瓶頸，並使其成為安全執行緒，讓它可在多執行緒重新計算 (MTR) 的所有可用執行緒上計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-841">We removed bottlenecks in its underlying memory and data structures as well as made it thread-safe to allow  it to be calculated on all available threads of Multithreaded recalculation (MTR).</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-842">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-842">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-843">**在 Outlook 中撰寫郵件時有新的選項可停用 @ 提及建議：** 您是否覺得 @ 提及的選擇器很煩人，一點都不好用？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-843">**New option to disable @ mention suggestions when composing mail in Outlook:** Do you find the @ mention picker more annoying than useful?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-844">現在您可以視需要將其關閉了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-844">Now you can turn it off if you prefer.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-845">在[部落格文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)中查看詳細資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-845">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/26/feedback-in-action-disable-mentions/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-846">**IT 系統管理員的事件通知：** Microsoft 365 租用戶全域系統管理員和 Office 應用程式系統會在 Windows 版 Outlook 的新右側面板中收到影響其使用者的 Outlook 和 O365 Exchange 事件通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-846">**Incident Notification for IT Admins:** Microsoft 365 tenant global administrators and Office Apps Administrators will be notified about Outlook and O365 Exchange incidents affecting their users with a new right-side panel notification in Outlook for Windows.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="8b21c-847">深入了解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-847">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/46c07f08-1277-41ce-b353-4e205e9da333)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-849">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-849">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-850">**改善的 PowerPoint 中的 Steam 影片效能：** 我們改善了 Microsoft Stream 影片的播放效能，將影片載入時間減至最少，以建立出流暢的觀賞體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-850">**Improved Stream video performance in PowerPoint:** We’ve made improvements to the playback performance of Microsoft Stream videos to minimize video loading time and create a smooth viewing experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-851">您可以在 Microsoft Stream 上使用公司影片來建立更完善的簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-851">Use your corporate videos from Microsoft Stream to create better presentations.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-852">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-852">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-853">**針對外部使用者遮罩 PSTN 參與者電話號碼：** 針對為其 Teams 會議啟用音訊會議的客戶，我們會對從組織外部加入的使用者，將 PSTN 參與者的電話號碼遮罩起來。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-853">**PSTN participant phone numbers are masked from external users:** For customers with Audio Conferencing enabled for their Teams meetings, we will mask the PSTN participant's phone number to users who have joined from outside of your organization.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-854">**管理您的頻道通知設定的簡化方式：** 透過團隊和頻道清單或從頻道標頭，使用者只要按一下即可將所有活動開啟或關閉就能快速管理其通知設定，或深入了解自訂以快速設定其偏好的通知排列組合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-854">**Simplified way to manage your channel notification settings:** Through the teams and channels list or from the channel header, the users can quickly manage their notification settings by turning all activity on or off with a single click or diving deep into custom to set their preferred permutations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-855">**Walkie Talkie：** 使用按著即可發言即時語音通訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-855">**Walkie Talkie:** Instant voice communication using push-to-talk.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-856">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-856">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-857">**螢幕閱讀器的動作確認：** 確認動作是重要的協助工具要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-857">**Confirmation of action in screen readers:** Confirmation of action is an important accessibility requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-858">隨著 Windows 引入新的通知 API 之後，我們現在就能通知螢幕助讀程式使用者的動作成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-858">With the introduction of a new Notification API from Windows, we are now able to alert screen reader users about the success of their actions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-859">[剪下]、[複製]、[貼上]、[粗體]、[畫底線]、[復原]、[重做]、[自動校正] 和 [自動大小寫] 等功能都已公布給 Win32 Word 的朗讀程式使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-859">Cut, copy, paste, bold, italic, underline, undo, redo, auto corrections, and auto-capitalizations are now all announced to Narrator users in Win32 Word.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-860">若要啟用此功能，請按 windows + ctrl + enter 以開啟朗讀程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-860">To enable this feature, turn on Narrator by pressing windows + ctrl + enter.</span></span>

### <a name="teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-962">Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-962">Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-963">**對 Teams 會議中視訊版面配置所做的變更：** 在 Teams 會議期間可同時檢視的參與者人數，很快地將從 4 個增加到 9 個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-963">**Changes to video layout in Teams meetings:** Soon, the number of participants that can be viewed simultaneously during a Teams meeting will increase from 4 to 9.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-964">**在即時活動中包含系統音訊：** 即時活動中的簡報者和製作人，現在可以在即時活動期間共用桌面或視窗螢幕時包含系統音訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-964">**Include system audio in live events:** Presenters and producers in live events can now include system audio when sharing a desktop or window screen during the live event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-965">這可讓您的使用者聽到您正在共用內容的任何音訊部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-965">This will allow your users to hear any audio part of the content you are sharing.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-966">**讓召集人可以變更撥入參與者的大廳設定：** 此設定會控制透過電話撥入的人員是否直接加入會議，或是在大廳中等候，而不論 [自動准許人員] 的設定為何。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-966">**Enable organizers to change lobby settings for dial-in participants:** This setting controls whether people who dial in by phone join the meeting directly or wait in the lobby regardless of the Automatically admit people setting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-967">**在會議中舉手：** 使用者現在可以在會議中虛擬舉手！</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-967">**Raise Your Hand in Meetings:** Users can now raise a virtual hand in a meeting!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-968">其他參與者會在會議舞台中您的名稱旁和名冊中您的名字旁看到您的舉手。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-968">Other participants will see your raised hand next to your name in the meeting stage and next to your name in the roster.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-969">**自訂會議視訊背景：** 使用視訊會議時，您現在可以選擇要使用的不同靜態背景影像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-969">**Customize meeting video backgrounds:** When you are meeting with video, you now have the choice of different static background images to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-970">這可讓您顯示此影像，而不是您所在位置的實際背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-970">This will let you show this image and not the actual background of where you are sitting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-971">**新增更多人員至聊天：** 我們現在可以將最多 350 個人新增至單一聊天對話。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-971">**Add more people to chat:** We made it possible to now add up to 350 people to a single chat thread.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-972">**您的活動摘要上設定齒輪：** 使用者現在可以從摘要左側滑軌透過設定齒輪的方式，直接存取活動摘要和通知設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-972">**Settings Gear on your Activity Feed:** Users can now directly access activity feed and notification setting from the feed left rail by the means of a settings gear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-973">**從 Teams 進行中的會議內輕鬆存取會議選項：** 我們讓會議召集人在 Teams 會議一開始，便能更快速且輕鬆地變更簡報者和大廳設定，方法是在參與者窗格中直接提供易於存取的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-973">**Easily access meeting options from within a Teams meeting in progress:** We are making it easier for meeting organizers to quickly and easily change their presenter and lobby settings once a Teams meeting starts by providing an easy to access link directly in the participants pane.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-974">此新功能將會同時對已排定和「立即開會」會議呈現。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-974">This new functionality will be present for both scheduled and “Meet Now” meetings.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-975">**團隊與頻道分析**：除了團隊分析以外，您現在也可以檢視頻道層級指標和深入資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-975">**Team and channel analytics:** In addition to team analytics, now you can also view channel level metrics and insights.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-976">我們也將時間週期增加到 90 天，使得您可以分析資料的時間較長。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-976">We've also enhanced the time period to 90 days so you can analyze data for longer periods.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-977">除此以外，此版本還包含有關小組或頻道的文章、回覆和會議計數的新計量和圖表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-977">Apart from that, this release also includes new metrics and charts around count of posts, replies and meetings for a team or channel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-978">**進入/結束宣告：** 我們新增了此功能，讓會議召集人能夠開啟或關閉會議的進入和結束宣告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-978">**Entry/exit announcements:** We added this feature that lets meeting organizers have the ability to turn on or off entry and exit announcements for a meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-990">解決會導致 Windows 10 伺服器版本的使用者看到警告「防毒軟體狀態: 無效」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-990">Addressed an issue that caused users of Windows 10 server versions to see the warning "Antivirus status: Invalid".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-991">此版本的 Windows 支援防毒軟體偵測，但即使已正確安裝防毒軟體，也找不到防毒軟體。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-991">This version of Windows supports antivirus detection, but no antivirus was found despite having anti virus correctly installed.</span></span>

### <a name="skype"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-993">Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-993">Skype</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-994">當使用者收到將他們移至 Teams Only 的原則時，他們仍然可以使用商務版 Skype Outlook 增益集來排程會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-994">When a user is given a policy that moves them to Teams Only, they were still able to use the Skype for Business Outlook add-in to schedule meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-995">在此更新之後，當客戶端讀取指示用戶為 Teams Only 的策略並進入僅限會議加入模式後，您將不再能用商務版 Skype 安排會議。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-995">After this update, you will no longer be able to schedule Skype for Business meetings after the client reads the policy indicating the user is Teams Only, and enters meeting join only mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-996">此外，如果商務版 Skype Outlook 增益集發現商務版 Skype 用戶端處於 [僅限會議加入] 模式，就無法自行啟動。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-996">Additionally the Skype for Business Outlook Add-in will not activate itself while starting up if it sees the Skype for Business client is in meeting join only mode.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="8b21c-997">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-997">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-998">此更新修正了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 中的問題，其中特定 VBA 專案參考了程式庫名稱或程式庫路徑中有 DBCS 字元的程式碼程式庫，因而在載入時被 Office 應用程式視為損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-998">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-999">此更新解決了 Microsoft Office 中的一個問題：可能無法在執行時期正確找到 Visual Basic for Applications 專案，這些專案的參照預期透搜尋 PATH 環境變數指定的位置來找到，進而導致VBA 執行時期錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-999">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-1000">當您啟用增益集，而登錄金鑰 HKEY_CURRENT_USER \Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth 被設為零時，辦公主機視窗會當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-1000">The office host was crashing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-1001">這變更將修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-1001">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-1280">解決在某些情況下，導致使用者看到電子郵件傳送到與顯示的 SMTP 位址不相符之地址的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-1280">Addressed an issue that caused users to see emails sent to an address that did not match the displayed SMTP address in some circumstances.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="8b21c-1281">解決在擷取雲端設定時，導致使用者在 Outlook 中遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8b21c-1281">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience hangs in Outlook when retrieving Cloud Settings.</span></span>
